Really happy for Hayden. I was 23 when Attack of the Clones came out, and even then (before social media), I thought the dude was getting a raw deal with how fans (& my own friends) were reacting. But man, I loved him in Revenge of the Sith - that movie like most still had issues, but it certainly had nothing to do with him.
